               \n                    Nicholas Bostick                \n            \n                                    Like a Latin Laurel and Hardy, Enrique Iglesias and Pitbull are an entertaining odd couple who have dominated music charts on both sides of the border. The King of Latin Pop, Iglesias, has sold more than 140 million records worldwide in his career while Mr. Worldwide, Putbull, just released his 10th studio album, Climate Change, which features Iglesias. But what makes this duo even more interesting is the contrasting styles.
